#
# TABLE STRUCTURE FOR: data_jamaah
#

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS data_jamaah;

CREATE TABLE `data_jamaah` (
  `id_jamaah` bigint(20) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `tahun` year(4) NOT NULL,
  `id_status` int(5) NOT NULL DEFAULT '2',
  `bank` varchar(50) COLLATE latin1_general_ci NOT NULL,
  `nama_jamaah` varchar(25) COLLATE latin1_general_ci NOT NULL,
  `kelengkapan` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `layanan` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1',
  `nama_ortu` varchar(20) COLLATE latin1_general_ci NOT NULL,
  `alamat_ktp` varchar(255) COLLATE latin1_general_ci NOT NULL,
  `alamat_jamaah` varchar(255) COLLATE latin1_general_ci NOT NULL,
  `no_tlp` varchar(40) COLLATE latin1_general_ci NOT NULL,
  `hp` varbinary(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `id_kecamatan` int(25) NOT NULL,
  `id_kabupaten` int(25) NOT NULL,
  `no_rekening` varchar(20) COLLATE latin1_general_ci NOT NULL,
  `no_porsi` varchar(20) COLLATE latin1_general_ci NOT NULL,
  `tgl_daftar` date NOT NULL,
  `tgl_porsi` date NOT NULL,
  `tgl_tempo` date NOT NULL,
  `foto` varchar(255) COLLATE latin1_general_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `porsi` varchar(255) COLLATE latin1_general_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `spph` varchar(255) COLLATE latin1_general_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `kartukeluarga` varchar(255) COLLATE latin1_general_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `ktp` varchar(255) COLLATE latin1_general_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `surat_nikah` varchar(255) COLLATE latin1_general_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `setoran_awal_bpih` varchar(255) COLLATE latin1_general_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `keterangan` text COLLATE latin1_general_ci,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id_jamaah`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM AUTO_INCREMENT=1771 DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 COLLATE=latin1_general_ci;
